\\t// PrevRunAddr is the absolute address that this resource instance had at\\n220: \\t// the conclusion of a previous run.\\n221: \\t//\\n222: \\t// This will typically be the same as Addr, but can be different if the\\n223: \\t// previous resource instance was subject to a \\\"moved\\\" block that we\\n224: \\t// handled in the process of creating this plan.\\n225: \\t//\\n226: \\t// For the In that case,\\n238: \\t// DeposedKey in the plan is always states.NotDeposed, representing that\\n239: \\t// the current object is being replaced with the deposed.\\n240: \\tDeposedKey states.DeposedKey\\n241: \\n242: \\t// Provider is the address of the provider configuration that was used\\n243: \\t// to plan this change, and thus the configuration that must also be\\n244: \\t// used to apply it.\\n245: \\tProviderAddr addrs.AbsProviderConfig\\n246: \\n247: \\t// Change is an embedded description of the change.\\n248: \\tChange\\n249: \\n250: \\t// ActionReason is an optional extra indication of why we chose the\\n251: \\t// action recorded in Change.Action for this particular resource instance.\\n252: \\t//\\n253: \\t// This is an approximate mechanism only for the purpose of explaining the\\n254: \\t// plan to end-users in the UI and is not to be used for any\\n255: \\t// decision-making during the apply step; if apply behavior needs to vary\\n256: \\t// depending on the \\\"action reason\\\" then the information for that decision\\n257: \\t// must be recorded more precisely elsewhere for that purpose.\\n258: \\t//\\n259: \\t// Sometimes there might be more than one reason for choosing a particular\\n260: \\t// action. Pass the implied type of the\\n282: // corresponding resource type schema for correct operation.\\n283: func (rc *ResourceInstanceChange) Encode(ty cty.Type) (*ResourceInstanceChangeSrc, error) {\\n284: \\tcs, err := rc.Change.Encode(ty)\\n285: \\tif err != nil {\\n286: \\t\\treturn nil, err\\n287: \\t}\\n288: \\tprevRunAddr := rc.PrevRunAddr\\n289: \\tif prevRunAddr.Resource.Resource.Type == \\\"\\\" {\\n290: \\t\\t// Suggests an old caller that hasn't been properly updated to\\n291: \\t\\t// populate this yet.\\n292: \\t\\tprevRunAddr = rc.Addr\\n293: \\t}\\n294: \\treturn &ResourceInstanceChangeSrc{\\n295: \\t\\tAddr:            rc.Addr,\\n296: \\t\\tPrevRunAddr:     prevRunAddr,\\n297: \\t\\tDeposedKey:      rc.DeposedKey,\\n298: \\t\\tProviderAddr:    rc.ProviderAddr,\\n299: \\t\\tChangeSrc:       *cs,\\n300: \\t\\tActionReason:    rc.ActionReason,\\n301: \\t\\tRequiredReplace: rc.RequiredReplace,\\n302: \\t\\tPrivate:         rc.Private,\\n303: \\t}, err\\n304: }\\n305: \\n306: func (rc *ResourceInstanceChange) DeepCopy() *ResourceInstanceChange {\\n307: \\tif rc == nil {\\n308: \\t\\treturn rc\\n309: \\t}\\n310: \\n311: \\tret := *rc\\n312: \\treturn &ret\\n313: }\\n314: \\n315: func (rc *ResourceInstanceChange) Moved() bool {\\n316: \\treturn !rc.Addr.Equal(rc.PrevRunAddr)\\n317: }\\n318: \\n319: // Simplify will, where possible, produce a change with a simpler action than\\n320: // the receiever given a flag indicating whether the caller is dealing with\\n321: // a normal apply or a destroy. Pass the type constraint\\n603: // that the values are expected to conform to; to properly decode the values\\n604: // later an identical type constraint must be provided at that time.\\n605: //\\n606: // Where a Change is embedded in some other struct, it's generally better\\n607: // to call the corresponding Encode method of that struct rather than working\\n608: // directly with its embedded Change.\\n609: func (c *Change) Encode(ty cty.Type) (*ChangeSrc, error) {\\n610: \\t// We can't serialize value marks directly so we'll need to extract the\\n611: \\t// sensitive marks and store them in a separate field.\\n612: \\t//\\n613: \\t// We don't accept any other marks here. Encode(schemas *schemarepo.Schemas) (*ChangesSrc, error) {\n43: \t// a plan is always built even when there are errors, so make sure to return\n44: \t// a valid changesSrc.\n45: \tchangesSrc := ResourceInstanceChange describes a change to a particular resource instance\n213: // object.\n214: type ResourceInstanceChange struct {\n215: \t// Addr is the absolute address of the resource instance that the change\n216: \t// will apply to.\n217: \tAddr addrs.AbsResourceInstance\n218: \n219: \t// PrevRunAddr is the absolute address that this resource instance had at\n220: \t// the conclusion of a In that case, it's up to the codepath making that decision to\n261: \t// decide which value would provide the most relevant explanation to the\n262: \t// end-user and return that. It's not a goal of this field to represent\n263: \t// fine details about the planning process.\n264: \tActionReason ResourceInstanceChangeActionReason\n265: \n266: \t// RequiredReplace is a set of paths that caused the change action to be\n267: \t// Replace rather than Update. rc\n405: }\n406: \n407: // ResourceInstanceChangeActionReason allows for some extra user-facing\n408: // reasoning for why a particular change action was chosen for a particular\n409: // resource &ImportingSrc{\n557: \t\t\tID: i.ID.AsString(),\n558: \t\t}\n559: \t}\n560: \treturn &ImportingSrc{\n561: \t\tUnknown: true,\n562: \t}\n563: }\n564: \n565: // Change describes a single change with a given action.\n566: type Change struct {\n567: \t// Action defines what kind of change is being made.\n568: \tAction Action\n569: \n570: \t// Interpretation of Before and After depend on Action:\n571: \t//\n572: \t//     NoOp     Before and After are the same, unchanged value\n573: \t//     Create   Before is nil, and After is the expected value after create.\n574: \t//     Read     Before is any prior value (nil if no prior), and After is the\n575: \t//              value that was or will be read.\n576: \t//     Update   Before is the value prior to update, and After is the expected\n577: \t//              value after update.\n578: \t//     Replace  As with Update.\n579: \t//     Delete   Before is the value prior to delete, and After is always nil.\n580: \t//     Forget   As with Delete.\n581: \t//\n582: \t// Unknown values may appear anywhere within the Before and After values,\n583: \t// either as the values themselves or as nested elements within known\n584: \t// collections/structures.\n585: \tBefore, After cty.Value\n586: \n587: \t// Importing is present if the resource is being imported as part of this\n588: \t// change.\n589: \t//\n590: \t// Use the simple presence of this field to detect if a ChangeSrc is to be\n591: \t// imported, the contents of this structure may be modified going forward.\n592: \tImporting *Importing\n593: \n594: \t// GeneratedConfig contains any HCL config generated for this resource\n595: \t// during planning, as a string. If GeneratedConfig is populated, Importing\n596: \t// should be true. However, not all Importing changes contain generated\n597: \t// config.\n598: \tGeneratedConfig string\n599: }\n600: \n601: // Encode produces a variant of the reciever that has its change values\n602: // serialized so it can be written to a plan file. Pass the type constraint\n603: // that the values are expected to conform to; to properly decode the values\n604: // later an identical type constraint must be provided at that time.\n605: //\n606: // Where a Change is embedded in some other struct, it's generally better\n607: // to call the corresponding Encode method of that struct rather than working\n608: // directly with its embedded Change.\n609: func (c *Change) Encode(ty cty.Type) (*ChangeSrc, error) {\n610: \t// We can't serialize value marks directly so we'll need to extract the\n611: \t// sensitive marks and store them in a separate field.\n612: \t//\n613: \t// We don't accept any other marks here. The caller should have dealt\n614: \t// with those somehow and replaced them with unmarked placeholders before\n615: \t// writing the value into the state.\n616: \tunmarkedBefore, marksesBefore := c.Before.UnmarkDeepWithPaths()\n617: \tunmarkedAfter, marksesAfter := c.After.UnmarkDeepWithPaths()\n618: \tsensitiveAttrsBefore, unsupportedMarksesBefore := marks.PathsWithMark(marksesBefore, marks.Sensitive)\n619: \tsensitiveAttrsAfter, unsupportedMarksesAfter := marks.PathsWithMark(marksesAfter, marks.Sensitive)\n620: \tif len(unsupportedMarksesBefore) != 0 {\n621: \t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\n622: \t\t\t\"prior value %s: can't serialize value marked with %#v (this is a bug in Terraform)\",\n623: \t\t\ttfdiags.FormatCtyPath(unsupportedMarksesBefore[0].Path),\n624: \t\t\tunsupportedMarksesBefore[0].Marks,\n625: \t\t)\n626: \t}\n627: \tif len(unsupportedMarksesAfter) != 0 {\n628: \t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\n629: \t\t\t\"new value %s: can't serialize value marked with %#v (this is a bug in Terraform)\",\n630: \t\t\ttfdiags.FormatCtyPath(unsupportedMarksesAfter[0].Path),\n631: \t\t\tunsupportedMarksesAfter[0].Marks,\n632: \t\t)\n633: \t}\n634: \n635: \tbeforeDV, err := NewDynamicValue(unmarkedBefore, ty)\n636: \tif err != nil {\n637: \t\treturn nil, err\n638: \t}\n639: \tafterDV, err := NewDynamicValue(unmarkedAfter, ty)\n640: \tif err != nil {\n641: \t\treturn nil, err\n642: \t}\n643: \n644: \treturn &ChangeSrc{\n645: \t\tAction:               c.Action,\n646: \t\tBefore:               beforeDV,\n647: \t\tAfter:                afterDV,\n648: \t\tBeforeSensitivePaths: sensitiveAttrsBefore,\n649: \t\tAfterSensitivePaths:  sensitiveAttrsAfter,\n650: \t\tImporting:            c.Importing.Encode(),\n651: \t\tGeneratedConfig:      c.GeneratedConfig,\n652: \t}, nil\n653: }\n654: ","url":"https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/github.com/sg-evals/terraform--v1.10.3@9802216fb24076bc614d9fa7961a9d85f6d7ec48/-/blob/internal/plans/changes.go"}}}

Copyright (c) HashiCorp, Inc.\n// SPDX-License-Identifier: BUSL-1.1\n\npackage format\n\nimport (\n\t\"fmt\"\n\t\"sort\"\n\t\"strings\"\n\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/plans\"\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/schemarepo\"\n)\n\n// CompactDiffFormatter formats a plan as a condensed, summary-style diff\n// showing only resource-level changes without attribute-level detail.\ntype CompactDiffFormatter struct{}\n\n// Format produces a compact summary of the given plan, showing one line per\n// resource change grouped by action type, followed by a summary count.\nfunc (f *CompactDiffFormatter) Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *schemarepo.Schemas) string {\n\tif plan == nil || plan.Changes == nil {\n\t\treturn \"No changes.\\n\"\n\t}\n\n\tchanges := plan.Changes.Resources\n\tif len(changes) == 0 {\n\t\treturn \"No changes.\\n\"\n\t}\n\n\t// Group changes by action type\n\tgrouped := make(map[plans.Action][]string)\n\tfor _, rc := range changes {\n\t\tif rc.Action == plans.NoOp {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\taddr := rc.Addr.String()\n\t\tgrouped[rc.Action] = append(grouped[rc.Action], addr)\n\t}\n\n\tif len(grouped) == 0 {\n\t\treturn \"No changes.\\n\"\n\t}\n\n\t// Define action display order\n\tactionOrder := []plans.Action{\n\t\tplans.Create,\n\t\tplans.Update,\n\t\tplans.DeleteThenCreate,\n\t\tplans.CreateThenDelete,\n\t\tplans.Delete,\n\t\tplans.Forget,\n\t\tplans.CreateThenForget,\n\t\tplans.Read,\n\t}\n\n\tvar buf strings.Builder\n\tvar summaryParts []string\n\n\tfor _, action := range actionOrder {\n\t\taddrs, ok := grouped[action]\n\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\tsort.Strings(addrs)\n\t\tlabel := actionLabel(action)\n\t\tfor _, addr := range addrs {\n\t\t\tfmt.Fprintf(&buf, \"[%s] %s\\n\", label, addr)\n\t\t}\n\t\tsummaryParts = append(summaryParts, fmt.Sprintf(\"%d to %s\", len(addrs), label))\n\t}\n\n\tbuf.WriteString(\"\\n\")\n\tfmt.Fprintf(&buf, \"Plan: %s.\\n\", strings.Join(summaryParts, \", \"))\n\n\treturn buf.String()\n}\n\nfunc actionLabel(action plans.Action) string {\n\tswitch action {\n\tcase plans.Create:\n\t\treturn \"create\"\n\tcase plans.Update:\n\t\treturn \"update\"\n\tcase plans.DeleteThenCreate:\n\t\treturn \"replace (delete then create)\"\n\tcase plans.CreateThenDelete:\n\t\treturn \"replace (create then delete)\"\n\tcase plans.Delete:\n\t\treturn \"delete\"\n\tcase plans.Forget:\n\t\treturn \"forget\"\n\tcase plans.CreateThenForget:\n\t\treturn \"create then forget\"\n\tcase plans.Read:\n\t\treturn \"read\"\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn \"change\"\n\t}\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
